[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-driven libFuzzer run of the `ExpanderFuzzer` on the Apache Commons [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompress “Expander” example triggered a Java heap space OutOfMemoryError within the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLZW decompression routine. The fuzzer reported a low-severity security issue [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m“FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when processing a crafted input file.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzzing of the `ExpanderFuzzer` harness, the target application crashed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a Java `OutOfMemoryError` while initializing the LZW decoding tables in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.lzw.LZWInputStream`. Jazzer classified the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash as a low-severity security issue due to memory exhaustion.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This behavior corresponds to a resource exhaustion vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenial of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mservice[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the decompression code path.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Observations and Findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The crash stack trace pinpoints the failure in  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLZWInputStream.jav[0m[1;92ma:186[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Propagating through `ZCompressorInputStream` and the generic [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorStreamFactory`.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Finally invoked by the `Expander.decompress` method used by the fuzzer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The fuzzer settings included a memory limit flag [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-[0m[33mrss_limit_mb[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m2560[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimeout, but no explicit maximum heap size override, leading to the default heap [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimit being hit.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Jazzer instrumentation covered a wide range of compressor and I/O classes [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mgzip, bzip2, xz, zstandard, LZMA, pack200, snappy, deflate, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, confirming that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe crash is isolated to the LZW decompression path.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The libFuzzer harness entry point is `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich reads the entire input and feeds it to `Expander.expand`.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To gain a comprehensive view of the issue, the following components should be [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m96[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m98[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m[1;92ma[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m:75[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m89[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:        final int firstByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:        final int secondByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:        final int thirdByte = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35min.readBits[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfirstByte != MAGIC_1 || secondByte != MAGIC_2 || thirdByte < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Input is not in .Z format"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        blockMode = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthirdByte & BLOCK_MODE_MASK[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:        maxCodeSize = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mblockMode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35msetClearCode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDEFAULT_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mclearEntries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/test/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStreamTest.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjav[0m[1;92ma:57[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m63[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:        final IntStream[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m invalid = [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mIntStream.range[0m[1;39m([0m[39mByte.MIN_VALUE, [0m[1;36m-120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mIntStream.range[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-97[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m-88[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mIntStream.range[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-65[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m-56[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mIntStream.range[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-33[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m-24[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mIntStream.range[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mIntStream.range[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m31[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Analysis and Root Cause  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Java `OutOfMemoryError` is triggered in LZW decompression when [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`maxCodeSize` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mderived from the third header byte of a “.Z” file[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is too large.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `ZCompressorInputStream`, we read the third byte, mask off the lower [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bits[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and pass that full value [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `initializeTables` allocates arrays of size `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize`. If [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`maxCodeSize` is, for example, [0m[1;36m25[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m, the allocation explodes and OOMs occur.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no upper bound on `maxCodeSize`, nor is a memory limit enforced [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault `memoryLimitInKiB` is −[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests for invalid bit‐widths already exist for `maxCodeSize < [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEFAULT_CODE_SIZE [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `maxCodeSize >= [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m`, but no bounds exist in the [0m[1;36m17[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrange.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must still reject `maxCodeSize < DEFAULT_CODE_SIZE` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandled by existing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`initializeTables` check[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must preserve the current test behaviors for negative header values and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues ≥[0m[1;36m31[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only `.Z` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLZW[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m streams must be altered—the fix does not touch harness code, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother compressors, or test code outside `ZCompressorInputStreamTest`.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch to `ZCompressorInputStream`  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Define a sane upper cap on LZW code size. [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits are common in classic[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLZW; choose [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m to maximize compatibility while bounding memory use.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int MIN_CODE_SIZE = DEFAULT_CODE_SIZE;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m9[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static final int MAX_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Immediately after extracting `maxCodeSize` from the header, insert a bounds [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck:  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      maxCodeSize = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < MIN_CODE_SIZE || maxCodeSize > MAX_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"maxCodeSize "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize + [0m[32m" is [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mout of bounds."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the call to `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged—this will still enforce the lower bound via its own checks and populate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe tables when within range.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Test Suite Updates  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Extend `[0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStreamTest.testInvalidMaxCodeSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to cover [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader‐bit values that yield `maxCodeSize` in [0m[1;36m17[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add an `[0m[1;35mIntStream.range[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m17[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in the array of invalid ranges so any [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`thirdByte` producing `maxCodeSize > [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m` triggers `IllegalArgumentException`.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Bounding `maxCodeSize` prevents exponential memory allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m17[0m[39m…[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminates the OOM risk reported by the fuzzer.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using `IllegalArgumentException` aligns with existing behavior for [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout‐of‐range code sizes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcaught by tests[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change only affects the `.Z` decompressor—and specifically rejects [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious or pathological headers—without touching harness/fuzzing logic or [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal dependencies.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Some extremely unconventional “.Z” archives that legitimately use codes >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any exist[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will no longer decompress; the library will throw at [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstruction time.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: Document the new limit in Javadoc for `ZCompressorInputStream` and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecommend re-encoding such archives with a lower code size or using a different [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtool.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Code Ranges to Patch and Test Updates  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Patch: [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma` around lines [0m[1;36m82[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m87[0m[39m.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test: [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/test/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStreamTest[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.java`, update the `invalid` ranges in `[0m[1;35mtestInvalidMaxCodeSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mharness, utility, or external[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are modified.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy ensures we address the resource exhaustion vulnerability without [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltering fuzzing harnesses or breaking backward compatibility for typical `.Z` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchives.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m[12/25/25 15:57:13][0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.END                      ]8;id=212801;file:///home/qqor/aixcc/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=888524;file:///home/qqor/aixcc/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mn evals: [1;36m2[0m, patch status: PatchStatus.SOUND[1m)[0m                                        [2m               [0m
